138→\n   139→    @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n   140→    @Override\n   141→    public void configure(Map<String, ?> configs) throws KafkaException {\n   142→        try {\n   143→ 208→\n   209→    @Override\n   210→    public ListenerName listenerName() {\n   211→        return listenerName;\n   212→    }\n   213→\n   214→    @Override\n   215→    public KafkaChannel 356→\n   357→    private Class<? extends AuthenticateCallbackHandler> clientCallbackHandlerClass() {\n   358→        switch (clientSaslMechanism) {\n   359→            case described in http://docs.oracle.com/javase/8/docs/technotes/guides/security/jgss/jgss-features.html:\n   369→    // \"To enable Java GSS to delegate to the native GSS library and its list of native mechanisms,\n   370→    // set the system property \"sun.security.jgss.native\" to true\"\n   371→    // \"In addition, when performing operations as a particular Subject, for example, Subject.doAs(...)\n   372→    // or Subject.doAsPrivileged(...), the to-be-used GSSCredential should be added to Subject's\n   373→    // private credential set. Otherwise, the GSS operations will fail since no credential is found.\"\n   374→    private void maybeAddNativeGssapiCredentials(Subject subject) {\n   375→        boolean usingNativeJgss = Boolean.getBoolean(GSS_NATIVE_PROP);\n   376→        if (usingNativeJgss && subject.getPrivateCredentials(GSSCredential.class).isEmpty()) {\n   377→\n   378→            final String servicePrincipal = SaslClientAuthenticator.firstPrincipal(subject);\n   379→            KerberosName kerberosName;\n   380→            try {\n   381→                kerberosName = KerberosName.parse(servicePrincipal);\n   382→            } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n   383→                throw new KafkaException(\"Principal has name with unexpected format \" + servicePrincipal);\n   384→            }\n   385→            final String servicePrincipalName = kerberosName.serviceName();\n   386→            final String serviceHostname = kerberosName.hostName();\n   387→\n   388→            try {\n   389→                GSSManager manager = gssManager();\n   390→                // This Oid is used to represent the Kerberos version 5 GSS-API mechanism. It is defined in\n   391→                // RFC 1964.\n   392→                Oid krb5Mechanism = new Oid(\"1.2.840.113554.1.2.2\");\n   393→                GSSName gssName = manager.createName(servicePrincipalName + \"@\" + serviceHostname, GSSName.NT_HOSTBASED_SERVICE);\n   394→                GSSCredential cred = manager.createCredential(gssName,\n   395→                        GSSContext.INDEFINITE_LIFETIME, krb5Mechanism, GSSCredential.ACCEPT_ONLY);\n   396→                subject.getPrivateCredentials().add(cred);\n   397→                log.info(\"Configured native GSSAPI private credentials for {}@{}\", serviceHostname, serviceHostname);\n   398→            } catch (GSSException ex) {\n   399→                log.warn(\"Cannot add private credential to subject; clients authentication may fail\", ex);\n   400→            }\n   401→        }\n   402→    }\n   403→\n   404→    // Visibility to override for testing\n   405→    protected GSSManager gssManager() {\n   406→        return GSSManager.getInstance();\n   407→    }\n   408→\n   409→    // Visibility for testing\n   410→    protected Subject subject(String saslMechanism) {\n   411→        return subjects.get(saslMechanism);\n   412→    }\n   413→}\n   414→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication with server mechanism \" + saslMechanism);\n   212→                }\n   213→            } catch (CompletionException e) {\n   214→                throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication with server mechanism \" + saslMechanism, e.getCause());\n   215→            }\n   216→        }\n   217→    }\n   218→\n   219→    private SaslServer createSaslKerberosServer(final AuthenticateCallbackHandler saslServerCallbackHandler, final Map<String, ?> configs, Subject subject) throws IOException {\n   220→        // server is using a JAAS-authenticated subject: determine service principal name and hostname from kafka server's subject.\n   221→        final String servicePrincipal = SaslClientAuthenticator.firstPrincipal(subject);\n   222→        KerberosName kerberosName;\n   223→        try {\n   224→            kerberosName = KerberosName.parse(servicePrincipal);\n   225→        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n   226→            throw new KafkaException(\"Principal has name with unexpected format \" + servicePrincipal);\n   227→        }\n   228→        final String servicePrincipalName = kerberosName.serviceName();\n   229→        final String serviceHostname = kerberosName.hostName();\n   230→\n   231→        LOG.debug(\"Creating SaslServer for {} with mechanism {}\", kerberosName, saslMechanism);\n   232→\n   233→        try {\n   234→            return SecurityManagerCompatibility.get().callAs(subject, () ->\n   235→                    Sasl.createSaslServer(saslMechanism, servicePrincipalName, serviceHostname, configs, saslServerCallbackHandler));\n   236→        } catch (CompletionException e) {\n   237→            throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication\", e.getCause());\n   238→        }\n   239→    }\n   240→\n   241→    /**\n   242→     * Evaluates client responses via `SaslServer.evaluateResponse` and returns the issued challenge to the client until\n   243→     * authentication succeeds or fails.\n   244→     *\n   245→     * The messages are sent and received as size delimited bytes that consists of a 4 byte network-ordered size N\n   246→     * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\n   247→     */\n   248→    @SuppressWarnings(\"fallthrough\")\n   249→    @Override\n   250→    public void authenticate() throws IOException {\n   251→        if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\n   252→            if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\n   253→                return;\n   254→\n   255→            if (saslServer != null && saslServer.isComplete()) {\n   256→                setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n   257→                return;\n   258→            }\n   259→\n   260→            // allocate on heap (as opposed to any socket server memory pool)\n   261→            if (netInBuffer == null) netInBuffer = new NetworkReceive(saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize, connectionId);\n   262→\n   263→            try {\n   264→                netInBuffer.readFrom(transportLayer);\n   265→            } catch (InvalidReceiveException e) {\n   266→                throw new SaslAuthenticationException(\"Failing SASL authentication due to invalid receive size\", e);\n   267→            }\n   268→            if (!netInBuffer.complete())\n   269→                return;\n   270→            netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n   271→        }\n   272→        byte[] clientToken = new byte[netInBuffer.payload().remaining()];\n   273→        netInBuffer.payload().get(clientToken, 0, clientToken.length);\n   274→        netInBuffer = null; // reset the networkReceive as we read all the data.\n   275→        try {\n   276→            switch (saslState) {\n   277→                case REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE:\n   278→                case HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST:\n   279→                case HANDSHAKE_REQUEST:\n   280→                case INITIAL_REQUEST:\n   281→                    handleKafkaRequest(clientToken);\n   282→                    break;\n   283→                case REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM:\n   284→                    throw new SaslAuthenticationException(reauthInfo.badMechanismErrorMessage);\n   285→                case AUTHENTICATE:\n   286→                    handleSaslToken(clientToken);\n   287→                    // When the authentication exchange is complete and no more tokens are expected from the client,\n   288→                    // update SASL state. Current SASL state will be updated when outgoing writes to the client complete.\n   289→                    if (saslServer.isComplete())\n   290→                        setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n   291→                    break;\n   292→                default:\n   293→                    break;\n   294→            }\n   295→        } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n   296→            // Exception will be propagated after response is sent to client\n   297→            setSaslState(SaslState.FAILED, e);\n   298→        } catch (Exception e) {\n   299→            // In the case of IOExceptions and other unexpected exceptions, fail immediately\n   300→            saslState = SaslState.FAILED;\n   301→            LOG.debug(\"Failed during {}: {}\", reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText(), e.getMessage());\n   302→            throw e;\n   303→        }\n   304→    }\n   305→\n   306→    @Override\n   307→    public KafkaPrincipal principal() {\n   308→        Optional<SSLSession> sslSession = transportLayer instanceof SslTransportLayer ?\n   309→                Optional.of(((SslTransportLayer) transportLayer).sslSession()) : Optional.empty();\n   310→        SaslAuthenticationContext context = new SaslAuthenticationContext(saslServer, securityProtocol,\n   311→                clientAddress(), listenerName.value(), sslSession);\n   312→        KafkaPrincipal principal = principalBuilder.build(context);\n   313→        if (ScramMechanism.isScram(saslMechanism) && Boolean.parseBoolean((String) saslServer.getNegotiatedProperty(ScramLoginModule.TOKEN_AUTH_CONFIG))) {\n   314→            principal.tokenAuthenticated(true);\n   315→        }\n   316→        return principal;\n   317→    }\n   318→\n   319→    @Override\n   320→    public Optional<KafkaPrincipalSerde> principalSerde() {\n   321→        return principalBuilder instanceof KafkaPrincipalSerde ? Optional.of((KafkaPrincipalSerde) principalBuilder) : Optional.empty();\n   322→    }\n   323→\n   324→    @Override\n   325→    public boolean complete() {\n   326→        return saslState == SaslState.COMPLETE;\n   327→    }\n   328→\n   329→    @Override\n   330→    public void handleAuthenticationFailure() throws IOException {\n   331→        sendAuthenticationFailureResponse();\n   332→    }\n   333→\n   334→    @Override\n   335→    public void close() throws IOException {\n   336→        if (principalBuilder instanceof Closeable)\n   337→            Utils.closeQuietly((Closeable) principalBuilder, \"principal builder\");\n   338→        if (saslServer != null)\n   339→            saslServer.dispose();\n   340→    }\n   341→\n   342→    @Override\n   343→    public void reauthenticate(ReauthenticationContext reauthenticationContext) throws IOException {\n   344→        NetworkReceive saslHandshakeReceive = reauthenticationContext.networkReceive();\n   345→        if (saslHandshakeReceive == null)\n   346→            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n   347→                    \"Invalid saslHandshakeReceive in server-side re-authentication context: null\");\n   348→        SaslServerAuthenticator previousSaslServerAuthenticator = (SaslServerAuthenticator) reauthenticationContext.previousAuthenticator();\n   349→        reauthInfo.reauthenticating(previousSaslServerAuthenticator.saslMechanism,\n   350→                previousSaslServerAuthenticator.principal(), reauthenticationContext.reauthenticationBeginNanos());\n   351→        previousSaslServerAuthenticator.close();\n   352→        netInBuffer = saslHandshakeReceive;\n   353→        LOG.debug(\"Beginning re-authentication: {}\", this);\n   354→        netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n   355→        setSaslState(SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE);\n   356→        authenticate();\n   357→    }\n   358→\n   359→    @Override\n   360→    public Long serverSessionExpirationTimeNanos() {\n   361→        return reauthInfo.sessionExpirationTimeNanos;\n   362→    }\n   363→\n   364→    @Override\n   365→    public Long reauthenticationLatencyMs() {\n   366→        return reauthInfo.reauthenticationLatencyMs();\n   367→    }\n   368→\n   369→    @Override\n   370→    public boolean connectedClientSupportsReauthentication() {\n   371→        return reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication;\n   372→    }\n   373→\n   374→    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState) {\n   375→        setSaslState(saslState, null);\n   376→    }\n   377→\n   378→    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState, AuthenticationException exception) {\n   379→        if (netOutBuffer != null && !netOutBuffer.completed()) {\n   380→            pendingSaslState = saslState;\n   381→            pendingException = exception;\n   382→        } else {\n   383→            this.saslState = saslState;\n   384→            LOG.debug(\"Set SASL server state to {} during {}\", saslState, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\n   385→            this.pendingSaslState = null;\n   386→            this.pendingException = null;\n   387→            if (exception != null)\n   388→                throw exception;\n   389→        }\n   390→    }\n   391→\n   392→    private boolean flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps() throws IOException {\n   393→        boolean flushedCompletely = flushNetOutBuffer();\n   394→        if (flushedCompletely) {\n   395→            transportLayer.removeInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n   396→            if (pendingSaslState != null)\n   397→                setSaslState(pendingSaslState, pendingException);\n   398→        } else\n   399→            transportLayer.addInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n   400→        return flushedCompletely;\n   401→    }\n   402→\n   403→    private boolean flushNetOutBuffer() throws IOException {\n   404→        if (!netOutBuffer.completed())\n   405→            netOutBuffer.writeTo(transportLayer);\n   406→        return netOutBuffer.completed();\n   407→    }\n   408→\n   409→    private InetAddress serverAddress() {\n   410→        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getLocalAddress();\n   411→    }\n   412→\n   413→    private InetAddress clientAddress() {\n   414→        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getInetAddress();\n   415→    }\n   416→\n   417→    private int clientPort() {\n   418→        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getPort();\n   419→    }\n   420→\n   421→    private void handleSaslToken(byte[] clientToken) throws IOException {\n   422→        if (!enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders) {\n   423→            byte[] response = saslServer.evaluateResponse(clientToken);\n   424→            if (saslServer.isComplete()) {\n   425→                reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n   426→                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating())\n   427→                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n   428→            }\n   429→            if (response != null) {\n   430→                netOutBuffer = ByteBufferSend.sizePrefixed(ByteBuffer.wrap(response));\n   431→                flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps();\n   432→            }\n   433→        } else {\n   434→            ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(clientToken);\n   435→            RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\n   436→            ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\n   437→            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n   438→                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n   439→            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n   440→            if (apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_AUTHENTICATE) {\n   441→                IllegalSaslStateException e = new IllegalSaslStateException(\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \" + apiKey + \" during SASL authentication.\");\n   442→                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, requestAndSize.request.getErrorResponse(e));\n   443→                throw e;\n   444→            }\n   445→            short version = header.apiVersion();\n   446→            if (!header.isApiVersionSupported()) {\n   447→                // We cannot create an error response if the request version of SaslAuthenticate is not supported\n   448→                // This should not normally occur since clients typically check supported versions using ApiVersionsRequest\n   449→                throw new UnsupportedVersionException(\"Version \" + version + \" is not supported for apiKey \" + apiKey);\n   450→            }\n   451→            /*\n   452→             * The client sends multiple SASL_AUTHENTICATE requests, and the client is known\n   453→             * to support the required version if any one of them indicates it supports that\n   454→             * version.\n   455→             */\n   456→            if (!reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication)\n   457→                reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication = version > 0;\n   458→            SaslAuthenticateRequest saslAuthenticateRequest = (SaslAuthenticateRequest) requestAndSize.request;\n   459→\n   460→            try {\n   461→                byte[] responseToken = saslServer.evaluateResponse(\n   462→                        Utils.copyArray(saslAuthenticateRequest.data().authBytes()));\n   463→                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating() && saslServer.isComplete())\n   464→                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n   465→                // For versions with SASL_AUTHENTICATE header, send a response to SASL_AUTHENTICATE request even if token is empty.\n   466→                byte[] responseBytes = responseToken == null ? new byte[0] : responseToken;\n   467→                long sessionLifetimeMs = !saslServer.isComplete() ? 0L\n   468→                        : reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n   469→                sendKafkaResponse(requestContext, new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n   470→                        new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n   471→                        .setErrorCode(Errors.NONE.code())\n   472→                        .setAuthBytes(responseBytes)\n   473→                        .setSessionLifetimeMs(sessionLifetimeMs)));\n   474→            } catch (SaslAuthenticationException e) {\n   475→                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext,\n   476→                        new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n   477→                                new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n   478→                                .setErrorCode(Errors.SASL_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED.code())\n   479→                                .setErrorMessage(e.getMessage())));\n   480→                throw e;\n   481→            } catch (SaslException e) {\n   482→                KerberosError kerberosError = KerberosError.fromException(e);\n   483→                if (kerberosError != null && kerberosError.retriable()) {\n   484→                    // Handle retriable Kerberos exceptions as I/O exceptions rather than authentication exceptions\n   485→                    throw e;\n   486→                } else {\n   487→                    // DO NOT include error message from the `SaslException` in the client response since it may\n   488→                    // contain sensitive data like the existence of the user.\n   489→                    String errorMessage = \"Authentication failed during \"\n   490→                            + reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText()\n   491→                            + \" due to invalid credentials with SASL mechanism \" + saslMechanism;\n   492→                    buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n   493→                            new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n   494→                            .setErrorCode(Errors.SASL_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED.code())\n   495→                            .setErrorMessage(errorMessage)));\n   496→                    throw new SaslAuthenticationException(errorMessage, e);\n   497→                }\n   498→            }\n   499→        }\n   500→    }\n   501→\n   502→    /**\n   503→     * @throws InvalidRequestException if the request is not in Kafka format or if the API key is invalid. Clients\n   504→     * that support SASL without support for KIP-43 (e.g. Kafka Clients 0.9.x) are in the former bucket - the first\n   505→     * packet such clients send is a GSSAPI token starting with 0x60.\n   506→     */\n   507→    private void handleKafkaRequest(byte[] requestBytes) throws IOException, AuthenticationException {\n   508→        try {\n   509→            ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(requestBytes);\n   510→            RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\n   511→            ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\n   512→\n   513→            // Raise an error prior to parsing if the api cannot be handled at this layer. This avoids\n   514→            // unnecessary exposure to some of the more complex schema types.\n   515→            if (apiKey != ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS && apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_HANDSHAKE)\n   516→                throw new InvalidRequestException(\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \" + apiKey + \" during SASL handshake.\");\n   517→\n   518→            LOG.debug(\"Handling Kafka request {} during {}\", apiKey, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\n   519→\n   520→            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n   521→                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n   522→            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n   523→\n   524→            // A valid Kafka request was received, we can now update the sasl state\n   525→            if (saslState == SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST)\n   526→                setSaslState(SaslState.HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST);\n   527→\n   528→            if (apiKey == ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS)\n   529→                handleApiVersionsRequest(requestContext, (ApiVersionsRequest) requestAndSize.request);\n   530→            else {\n   531→                String clientMechanism = handleHandshakeRequest(requestContext, (SaslHandshakeRequest) requestAndSize.request);\n   532→                if (!reauthInfo.reauthenticating() || reauthInfo.saslMechanismUnchanged(clientMechanism)) {\n   533→                    createSaslServer(clientMechanism);\n   534→                    setSaslState(SaslState.AUTHENTICATE);\n   535→                }\n   536→            }\n   537→        } catch (InvalidRequestException e) {\n   538→            if (saslState == SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST) {\n   539→                // InvalidRequestException is thrown if the request is not in Kafka format or if the API key is invalid.\n   540→                // If it's the initial request, this could be an ancient client (see method documentation for more details),\n   541→                // a client configured with the wrong security protocol or a non kafka-client altogether (eg http client).\n   542→                throw new InvalidRequestException(\"Invalid request, potential reasons: kafka client configured with the \" +\n   543→                    \"wrong security protocol, it does not support KIP-43 or it is not a kafka client.\", e);\n   544→            }\n   545→            throw e;\n   546→        }\n   547→    }\n   548→\n   549→    private String handleHandshakeRequest(RequestContext context, SaslHandshakeRequest handshakeRequest) throws IOException, UnsupportedSaslMechanismException {\n   550→        String clientMechanism = handshakeRequest.data().mechanism();\n   551→        short version = context.header.apiVersion();\n   552→        if (version >= 1)\n   553→            this.enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders(true);\n   554→        if (enabledMechanisms.contains(clientMechanism)) {\n   555→            LOG.debug(\"Using SASL mechanism '{}' provided by client\", clientMechanism);\n   556→            sendKafkaResponse(context, new SaslHandshakeResponse(\n   557→                    new SaslHandshakeResponseData().setErrorCode(Errors.NONE.code()).setMechanisms(enabledMechanisms)));\n   558→            return clientMechanism;\n   559→        } else {\n   560→            LOG.debug(\"SASL mechanism '{}' requested by client is not supported\", clientMechanism);\n   561→            buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(context, new SaslHandshakeResponse(\n   562→                    new SaslHandshakeResponseData().setErrorCode(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_SASL_MECHANISM.code()).setMechanisms(enabledMechanisms)));\n   563→            throw new UnsupportedSaslMechanismException(\"Unsupported SASL mechanism \" + clientMechanism);\n   564→        }\n   565→    }\n   566→\n   567→    // Visible to override for testing\n   568→    protected void enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders(boolean flag) {\n   569→        this.enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders = flag;\n   570→    }\n   571→\n   572→    private void handleApiVersionsRequest(RequestContext context, ApiVersionsRequest apiVersionsRequest) throws IOException {\n   573→        if (saslState != SaslState.HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST)\n   574→            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Unexpected ApiVersions request received during SASL authentication state \" + saslState);\n   575→\n   576→        if (apiVersionsRequest.hasUnsupportedRequestVersion())\n   577→            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionsRequest.getErrorResponse(0, Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION.exception()));\n   578→        else if (!apiVersionsRequest.isValid())\n   579→            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionsRequest.getErrorResponse(0, Errors.INVALID_REQUEST.exception()));\n   580→        else {\n   581→            metadataRegistry.registerClientInformation(new ClientInformation(apiVersionsRequest.data().clientSoftwareName(),\n   582→                apiVersionsRequest.data().clientSoftwareVersion()));\n   583→            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionSupplier.apply(apiVersionsRequest.version()));\n   584→            setSaslState(SaslState.HANDSHAKE_REQUEST);\n   585→        }\n   586→    }\n   587→\n   588→    /**\n   589→     * Build a {@link Send} response on {@link #authenticate()} failure. The actual response is sent out when\n   590→     * {@link #sendAuthenticationFailureResponse()} is called.\n   591→     */\n   592→    private void buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(RequestContext context, AbstractResponse response) {\n   593→        authenticationFailureSend = context.buildResponseSend(response);\n   594→    }\n   595→\n   596→    /**\n   597→     * Send any authentication failure response that may have been previously built.\n   598→     */\n   599→    private void sendAuthenticationFailureResponse() throws IOException {\n   600→        if (authenticationFailureSend == null)\n   601→            return;\n   602→        sendKafkaResponse(authenticationFailureSend);\n   603→        authenticationFailureSend = null;\n   604→    }\n   605→\n   606→    private void sendKafkaResponse(RequestContext context, AbstractResponse response) throws IOException {\n   607→        sendKafkaResponse(context.buildResponseSend(response));\n   608→    }\n   609→\n   610→    private void sendKafkaResponse(Send send) throws IOException {\n   611→        netOutBuffer = send;\n   612→        flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps();\n   613→    }\n   614→\n   615→    /**\n   616→     * Information related to re-authentication\n   617→     */\n   618→    private class ReauthInfo {\n   619→        public String previousSaslMechanism;\n   620→        public KafkaPrincipal previousKafkaPrincipal;\n   621→        public long reauthenticationBeginNanos;\n   622→        public Long sessionExpirationTimeNanos;\n   623→        public boolean connectedClientSupportsReauthentication;\n   624→        public long authenticationEndNanos;\n   625→        public String badMechanismErrorMessage;\n   626→\n   627→        public void reauthenticating(String previousSaslMechanism, KafkaPrincipal previousKafkaPrincipal,\n   628→                long reauthenticationBeginNanos) {\n   629→            this.previousSaslMechanism = Objects.requireNonNull(previousSaslMechanism);\n   630→            this.previousKafkaPrincipal = Objects.requireNonNull(previousKafkaPrincipal);\n   631→            this.reauthenticationBeginNanos = reauthenticationBeginNanos;\n   632→        }\n   633→\n   634→        public boolean reauthenticating() {\n   635→            return previousSaslMechanism != null;\n   636→        }\n   637→\n   638→        public String authenticationOrReauthenticationText() {\n   639→            return reauthenticating() ? \"re-authentication\" : \"authentication\";\n   640→        }\n   641→\n   642→        public void ensurePrincipalUnchanged(KafkaPrincipal reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal) throws SaslAuthenticationException {\n   643→            if (!previousKafkaPrincipal.equals(reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal)) {\n   644→                throw new SaslAuthenticationException(String.format(\n   645→                        \"Cannot change principals during re-authentication from %s.%s: %s.%s\",\n   646→                        previousKafkaPrincipal.getPrincipalType(), previousKafkaPrincipal.getName(),\n   647→                        reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal.getPrincipalType(), reauthenticatedKafkaPrincipal.getName()));\n   648→            }\n   649→        }\n   650→\n   651→        /*\n   652→         * We define the REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM state because the failed re-authentication\n   653→         * metric does not get updated if we send back an error immediately upon the\n   654→         * start of re-authentication.\n   655→         */\n   656→        public boolean saslMechanismUnchanged(String clientMechanism) {\n   657→            if (previousSaslMechanism.equals(clientMechanism))\n   658→                return true;\n   659→            badMechanismErrorMessage = String.format(\n   660→                    \"SASL mechanism '%s' requested by client is not supported for re-authentication of mechanism '%s'\",\n   661→                    clientMechanism, previousSaslMechanism);\n   662→            LOG.debug(badMechanismErrorMessage);\n   663→            setSaslState(SaslState.REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM);\n   664→            return false;\n   665→        }\n   666→\n   667→        private long calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs() {\n   668→            long retvalSessionLifetimeMs = 0L;\n   669→            long authenticationEndMs = time.milliseconds();\n   670→            authenticationEndNanos = time.nanoseconds();\n   671→            Long credentialExpirationMs = (Long) saslServer\n   672→                    .getNegotiatedProperty(SaslInternalConfigs.CREDENTIAL_LIFETIME_MS_SASL_NEGOTIATED_PROPERTY_KEY);\n   673→            Long connectionsMaxReauthMs = connectionsMaxReauthMsByMechanism.get(saslMechanism);\n   674→            boolean maxReauthSet = connectionsMaxReauthMs != null && connectionsMaxReauthMs > 0;\n   675→\n   676→            if (credentialExpirationMs != null || maxReauthSet) {\n   677→                if (credentialExpirationMs == null)\n   678→                    retvalSessionLifetimeMs = zeroIfNegative(connectionsMaxReauthMs);\n   679→                else if (!maxReauthSet)\n   680→                    retvalSessionLifetimeMs = zeroIfNegative(credentialExpirationMs - authenticationEndMs);\n   681→                else\n   682→                    retvalSessionLifetimeMs = zeroIfNegative(Math.min(credentialExpirationMs - authenticationEndMs, connectionsMaxReauthMs));\n   683→\n   684→                sessionExpirationTimeNanos = authenticationEndNanos + 1000 * 1000 * retvalSessionLifetimeMs;\n   685→            }\n   686→\n   687→            if (credentialExpirationMs != null) {\n   688→                LOG.debug(\n   689→                        \"Authentication complete; session max lifetime from broker config={} ms, credential expiration={} ({} ms); session expiration = {} ({} ms), sending {} ms to client\",\n   690→                        connectionsMaxReauthMs, new Date(credentialExpirationMs),\n   691→                        credentialExpirationMs - authenticationEndMs,\n   692→                        new Date(authenticationEndMs + retvalSessionLifetimeMs), retvalSessionLifetimeMs,\n   693→                        retvalSessionLifetimeMs);\n   694→            } else {\n   695→                if (sessionExpirationTimeNanos != null)\n   696→                    LOG.debug(\n   697→ channel on the server side starts with the state\n     * {@link #REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE}. It may then flow to\n     * {@link #REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM} before a transition to {@link #FAILED} if\n     * re-authentication is attempted with a mechanism different than the original\n     * one; INITIAL_REQUEST,               // May be SaslHandshake or ApiVersions for authentication\n        HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST, // May be SaslHandshake or ApiVersions\n        HANDSHAKE_REQUEST,             // After an ApiVersions request, next request must be SaslHandshake\n        AUTHENTICATE,                  // Authentication tokens (SaslHandshake v1 and above indicate SaslAuthenticate headers)\n        COMPLETE,                      // Authentication completed successfully\n        FAILED,                        // Authentication failed\n        REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE,      // Initial state for re-authentication, processes SASL handshake request\n        REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM,          // When re-authentication requested with wrong mechanism, generate exception\n    }\n\n     saslServer = createSaslKerberosServer(callbackHandler, configs, subject);\n        } else {\n            try {\n                saslServer = SecurityManagerCompatibility.get().callAs(subject, () saslMechanism, e.getCause());\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    private SaslServer createSaslKerberosServer(final AuthenticateCallbackHandler saslServerCallbackHandler, final Map<String, ?> configs, Subject subject) throws IOException {\n        // server is using a JAAS-authenticated subject: determine service principal name and hostname from kafka server's subject.\n        final } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {\n            throw new KafkaException(\"Principal has name with unexpected format \" + servicePrincipal);\n        }\n        final String servicePrincipalName =     try {\n            return SecurityManagerCompatibility.get().callAs(subject, () ->\n                    Sasl.createSaslServer(saslMechanism, servicePrincipalName, serviceHostname, configs, saslServerCallbackHandler));\n        } catch (CompletionException e) {\n            throw new SaslException(\"Kafka Server failed to create a SaslServer to interact with a client during session authentication\", e.getCause());\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Evaluates client responses via `SaslServer.evaluateResponse` and returns the issued challenge to the client until\n     * authentication succeeds or fails.\n     *\n     * The messages are sent and received as size delimited bytes that consists of a 4 byte network-ordered size N\n     * followed by N bytes representing the opaque payload.\n     */\n    @SuppressWarnings(\"fallthrough\")\n    @Override\n    public void authenticate() throws IOException {\n        if (saslState != SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE) {\n            if (netOutBuffer != null && !flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps())\n                return;\n\n            if (saslServer != null && saslServer.isComplete()) {\n                setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n                return;\n            }\n\n            // allocate on heap (as opposed to any socket server memory pool)\n            if (netInBuffer == null) netInBuffer = new NetworkReceive(saslAuthRequestMaxReceiveSize, connectionId);\n\n            try {\n                netInBuffer.readFrom(transportLayer);\n            } catch (InvalidReceiveException e) {\n                throw new SaslAuthenticationException(\"Failing SASL authentication due to invalid receive size\", e);\n            }\n            if (!netInBuffer.complete())\n                return;\n            netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n        }\n        byte[] clientToken = new byte[netInBuffer.payload().remaining()];\n        netInBuffer.payload().get(clientToken, 0, clientToken.length);\n        netInBuffer = null; // reset the networkReceive as we read all the data.\n        try {\n            switch (saslState) {\n                case REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE:\n                case HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST:\n                case HANDSHAKE_REQUEST:\n                case INITIAL_REQUEST:\n                    handleKafkaRequest(clientToken);\n                    break;\n                case REAUTH_BAD_MECHANISM:\n                    throw new SaslAuthenticationException(reauthInfo.badMechanismErrorMessage);\n                case AUTHENTICATE:\n                    handleSaslToken(clientToken);\n                    // When the authentication exchange is complete and no more tokens are expected from the client,\n                    // update SASL state. Current SASL state will be updated when outgoing writes to the client complete.\n                    if (saslServer.isComplete())\n                        setSaslState(SaslState.COMPLETE);\n                    break;\n                default:\n                    break;\n            }\n        } catch (AuthenticationException e) {\n            // Exception will be propagated after response is sent to client\n            setSaslState(SaslState.FAILED, e);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            // In the case of IOExceptions and other unexpected exceptions, fail immediately\n            saslState = SaslState.FAILED;\n            LOG.debug(\"Failed during {}: {}\", reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText(), e.getMessage());\n            throw e;\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public KafkaPrincipal principal() {\n        Optional<SSLSession> sslSession = transportLayer instanceof SslTransportLayer ?\n                Optional.of(((SslTransportLayer) transportLayer).sslSession()) : Optional.empty();\n        SaslAuthenticationContext context = new SaslAuthenticationContext(saslServer, securityProtocol,\n                clientAddress(), listenerName.value(), sslSession);\n        KafkaPrincipal principal = principalBuilder.build(context);\n        if (ScramMechanism.isScram(saslMechanism) && Boolean.parseBoolean((String) saslServer.getNegotiatedProperty(ScramLoginModule.TOKEN_AUTH_CONFIG))) {\n            principal.tokenAuthenticated(true);\n        }\n        return principal;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Optional<KafkaPrincipalSerde> principalSerde() {\n        return principalBuilder instanceof KafkaPrincipalSerde ? Optional.of((KafkaPrincipalSerde) principalBuilder) : Optional.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean complete() {\n        return saslState == SaslState.COMPLETE;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void handleAuthenticationFailure() throws IOException {\n        sendAuthenticationFailureResponse();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void close() throws IOException {\n        if (principalBuilder instanceof Closeable)\n            Utils.closeQuietly((Closeable) principalBuilder, \"principal builder\");\n        if (saslServer != null)\n            saslServer.dispose();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void reauthenticate(ReauthenticationContext reauthenticationContext) throws IOException {\n        NetworkReceive saslHandshakeReceive = reauthenticationContext.networkReceive();\n        if (saslHandshakeReceive == null)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\n                    \"Invalid saslHandshakeReceive in server-side re-authentication context: null\");\n        SaslServerAuthenticator previousSaslServerAuthenticator = (SaslServerAuthenticator) reauthenticationContext.previousAuthenticator();\n        reauthInfo.reauthenticating(previousSaslServerAuthenticator.saslMechanism,\n                previousSaslServerAuthenticator.principal(), reauthenticationContext.reauthenticationBeginNanos());\n        previousSaslServerAuthenticator.close();\n        netInBuffer = saslHandshakeReceive;\n        LOG.debug(\"Beginning re-authentication: {}\", this);\n        netInBuffer.payload().rewind();\n        setSaslState(SaslState.REAUTH_PROCESS_HANDSHAKE);\n        authenticate();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Long serverSessionExpirationTimeNanos() {\n        return public boolean connectedClientSupportsReauthentication() {\n        return reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication;\n    }\n\n    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState) {\n        setSaslState(saslState, null);\n    }\n\n    private void setSaslState(SaslState saslState, AuthenticationException exception) {\n        if (netOutBuffer != null && !netOutBuffer.completed()) {\n            pendingSaslState = saslState;\n            pendingException = exception;\n        } else {\n            this.saslState = saslState;\n            LOG.debug(\"Set SASL server state to {} during {}\", saslState, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\n            this.pendingSaslState = null;\n            this.pendingException = null;\n            if (exception != null)\n                throw exception;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private boolean flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps() throws IOException {\n        boolean flushedCompletely = flushNetOutBuffer();\n        if (flushedCompletely) {\n            transportLayer.removeInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n            if (pendingSaslState != null)\n                setSaslState(pendingSaslState, pendingException);\n        } else\n            transportLayer.addInterestOps(SelectionKey.OP_WRITE);\n        return flushedCompletely;\n    }\n\n    private boolean flushNetOutBuffer() throws IOException {\n        if (!netOutBuffer.completed())\n            netOutBuffer.writeTo(transportLayer);\n        return netOutBuffer.completed();\n    }\n\n    private InetAddress serverAddress() {\n        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getLocalAddress();\n    }\n\n    private InetAddress clientAddress() {\n        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getInetAddress();\n    }\n\n    private int clientPort() {\n        return transportLayer.socketChannel().socket().getPort();\n    }\n\n    private void handleSaslToken(byte[] clientToken) throws IOException {\n        if (!enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders) {\n            byte[] response = saslServer.evaluateResponse(clientToken);\n            if (saslServer.isComplete()) {\n                reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating())\n                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n            }\n            if (response != null) {\n                netOutBuffer = ByteBufferSend.sizePrefixed(ByteBuffer.wrap(response));\n                flushNetOutBufferAndUpdateInterestOps();\n            }\n        } else {\n            ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(clientToken);\n            RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\n            ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\n            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n            if (apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_AUTHENTICATE) {\n                IllegalSaslStateException e = new IllegalSaslStateException(\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \" + apiKey + \" during SASL authentication.\");\n                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, requestAndSize.request.getErrorResponse(e));\n                throw e;\n            }\n            short version = header.apiVersion();\n            if (!header.isApiVersionSupported()) {\n                // We cannot create an error response if the request version of SaslAuthenticate is not supported\n                // This should not normally occur since clients typically check supported versions using ApiVersionsRequest\n                throw new UnsupportedVersionException(\"Version \" + version + \" is not supported for apiKey \" + apiKey);\n            }\n            /*\n             * The client sends multiple SASL_AUTHENTICATE requests, and the client is known\n             * to support the required version if any one of them indicates it supports that\n             * version.\n             */\n            if (!reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication)\n                reauthInfo.connectedClientSupportsReauthentication = version > 0;\n            SaslAuthenticateRequest saslAuthenticateRequest = (SaslAuthenticateRequest) requestAndSize.request;\n\n            try {\n                byte[] responseToken = saslServer.evaluateResponse(\n                        Utils.copyArray(saslAuthenticateRequest.data().authBytes()));\n                if (reauthInfo.reauthenticating() && saslServer.isComplete())\n                    reauthInfo.ensurePrincipalUnchanged(principal());\n                // For versions with SASL_AUTHENTICATE header, send a response to SASL_AUTHENTICATE request even if token is empty.\n                byte[] responseBytes = responseToken == null ? new byte[0] : responseToken;\n                long sessionLifetimeMs = !saslServer.isComplete() ? 0L\n                        : reauthInfo.calcCompletionTimesAndReturnSessionLifetimeMs();\n                sendKafkaResponse(requestContext, new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n                        new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n                        .setErrorCode(Errors.NONE.code())\n                        .setAuthBytes(responseBytes)\n                        .setSessionLifetimeMs(sessionLifetimeMs)));\n            } catch (SaslAuthenticationException e) {\n                buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext,\n                        new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n                                new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n                                .setErrorCode(Errors.SASL_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED.code())\n                                .setErrorMessage(e.getMessage())));\n                throw e;\n            } catch (SaslException e) {\n                KerberosError kerberosError = KerberosError.fromException(e);\n                if (kerberosError != null && kerberosError.retriable()) {\n                    // Handle retriable Kerberos exceptions as I/O exceptions rather than authentication exceptions\n                    throw e;\n                } else {\n                    // DO NOT include error message from the `SaslException` in the client response since it may\n                    // contain sensitive data like the existence of the user.\n                    String errorMessage = \"Authentication failed during \"\n                            + reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText()\n                            + \" due to invalid credentials with SASL mechanism \" + saslMechanism;\n                    buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(requestContext, new SaslAuthenticateResponse(\n                            new SaslAuthenticateResponseData()\n                            .setErrorCode(Errors.SASL_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED.code())\n                            .setErrorMessage(errorMessage)));\n                    throw new SaslAuthenticationException(errorMessage, e);\n                }\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * @throws InvalidRequestException if the request is not in Kafka format or if the API key is invalid. Clients\n     * that support SASL without support for KIP-43 (e.g. Kafka Clients 0.9.x) are in the former bucket - the first\n     * packet such clients send is a GSSAPI token starting with 0x60.\n     */\n    private void handleKafkaRequest(byte[] requestBytes) throws IOException, AuthenticationException {\n        try {\n            ByteBuffer requestBuffer = ByteBuffer.wrap(requestBytes);\n            RequestHeader header = RequestHeader.parse(requestBuffer);\n            ApiKeys apiKey = header.apiKey();\n\n            // Raise an error prior to parsing if the api cannot be handled at this layer. This avoids\n            // unnecessary exposure to some of the more complex schema types.\n            if (apiKey != ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS && apiKey != ApiKeys.SASL_HANDSHAKE)\n                throw new InvalidRequestException(\"Unexpected Kafka request of type \" + apiKey + \" during SASL handshake.\");\n\n            LOG.debug(\"Handling Kafka request {} during {}\", apiKey, reauthInfo.authenticationOrReauthenticationText());\n\n            RequestContext requestContext = new RequestContext(header, connectionId, clientAddress(), Optional.of(clientPort()),\n                    KafkaPrincipal.ANONYMOUS, listenerName, securityProtocol, ClientInformation.EMPTY, false);\n            RequestAndSize requestAndSize = requestContext.parseRequest(requestBuffer);\n\n            // A valid Kafka request was received, we can now update the sasl state\n            if (saslState == SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST)\n                setSaslState(SaslState.HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST);\n\n            if (apiKey == ApiKeys.API_VERSIONS)\n                handleApiVersionsRequest(requestContext, (ApiVersionsRequest) requestAndSize.request);\n            else {\n                String clientMechanism = handleHandshakeRequest(requestContext, (SaslHandshakeRequest) requestAndSize.request);\n                if (!reauthInfo.reauthenticating() || reauthInfo.saslMechanismUnchanged(clientMechanism)) {\n                    createSaslServer(clientMechanism);\n                    setSaslState(SaslState.AUTHENTICATE);\n                }\n            }\n        } catch (InvalidRequestException e) {\n            if (saslState == SaslState.INITIAL_REQUEST) {\n                // InvalidRequestException is thrown if the request is not in Kafka format or if the API key is invalid.\n                // If it's the initial request, this could be an ancient client (see method documentation for more details),\n                // a client configured with the wrong security protocol or a non kafka-client altogether (eg http client).\n                throw new InvalidRequestException(\"Invalid request, potential reasons: kafka client configured with the \" +\n                    \"wrong security protocol, it does not support KIP-43 or it is not a kafka client.\", e);\n            }\n            throw e;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private String handleHandshakeRequest(RequestContext context, SaslHandshakeRequest handshakeRequest) throws IOException, UnsupportedSaslMechanismException {\n        String clientMechanism = handshakeRequest.data().mechanism();\n        short version = context.header.apiVersion();\n        if (version >= 1)\n            this.enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders(true);\n        if (enabledMechanisms.contains(clientMechanism)) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Using SASL mechanism '{}' provided by client\", clientMechanism);\n            sendKafkaResponse(context, new SaslHandshakeResponse(\n                    new SaslHandshakeResponseData().setErrorCode(Errors.NONE.code()).setMechanisms(enabledMechanisms)));\n            return clientMechanism;\n        } else {\n            LOG.debug(\"SASL mechanism '{}' requested by client is not supported\", clientMechanism);\n            buildResponseOnAuthenticateFailure(context, new SaslHandshakeResponse(\n                    new SaslHandshakeResponseData().setErrorCode(Errors.UNSUPPORTED_SASL_MECHANISM.code()).setMechanisms(enabledMechanisms)));\n            throw new UnsupportedSaslMechanismException(\"Unsupported SASL mechanism \" + clientMechanism);\n        }\n    }\n\n    // Visible to override for testing\n    protected void enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders(boolean flag) {\n        this.enableKafkaSaslAuthenticateHeaders = flag;\n    }\n\n    private void handleApiVersionsRequest(RequestContext context, ApiVersionsRequest apiVersionsRequest) throws IOException {\n        if (saslState != SaslState.HANDSHAKE_OR_VERSIONS_REQUEST)\n            throw new IllegalStateException(\"Unexpected ApiVersions request received during SASL authentication state \" + saslState);\n\n        if (apiVersionsRequest.hasUnsupportedRequestVersion())\n            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionsRequest.getErrorResponse(0, Errors.UNSUPPORTED_VERSION.exception()));\n        else if (!apiVersionsRequest.isValid())\n            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionsRequest.getErrorResponse(0, Errors.INVALID_REQUEST.exception()));\n        else {\n            metadataRegistry.registerClientInformation(new ClientInformation(apiVersionsRequest.data().clientSoftwareName(),\n                apiVersionsRequest.data().clientSoftwareVersion()));\n            sendKafkaResponse(context, apiVersionSupplier.apply(apiVersionsRequest.version()));\n            setSaslState(SaslState.HANDSHAKE_REQUEST);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Build a {@link Send} AbstractResponse response) {\n        authenticationFailureSend = context.buildResponseSend(response);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Send any authentication failure response that may have been previously .getNegotiatedProperty(SaslInternalConfigs.CREDENTIAL_LIFETIME_MS_SASL_NEGOTIATED_PROPERTY_KEY);\n            Long connectionsMaxReauthMs = connectionsMaxReauthMsByMechanism.get(saslMechanism);\n (credentialExpirationMs == null)\n                    retvalSessionLifetimeMs = zeroIfNegative(connectionsMaxReauthMs);\n                else if (!maxReauthSet)\n SaslAuthenticationException(\"Authentication failed: username not specified\");\n        }\n        if (password.isEmpty()) {\n            throw new SaslAuthenticationException(\"Authentication failed: password not specified\");\n        }\n\n        NameCallback nameCallback = new NameCallback(\"username\", username);\n        PlainAuthenticateCallback authenticateCallback = new \"[a-zA-Z0-9/+]\";\n        static final String BASE64 = String.format(\"(?:%s{4})*(?:%s{3}=|%s{2}==)?\", BASE64_CHAR, BASE64_CHAR, BASE64_CHAR);\n        static final String RESERVED = String.format(\"(m=%s,)?\", VALUE);\n        static final String EXTENSIONS = String.format(\"(,%s=%s)*\", ALPHA, VALUE);\n\n        abstract String toMessage();\n\n        public byte[] toBytes() {\n            return toMessage().getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);\n        }\n\n        protected String toMessage(byte[] messageBytes) {\n            return new String(messageBytes, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Format:\n     *     gs2-header [reserved-mext \",\"] username \",\" nonce [\",\" extensions]\n     * Limitations:\n     *     Only PATTERN = Pattern.compile(String.format(\n                \"n,(a=(?<authzid>%s))?,%sn=(?<saslname>%s),r=(?<nonce>%s)(?<extensions>%s)\",\n                SASLNAME,\n                RESERVED,\n                SASLNAME,\n                PRINTABLE,\n                EXTENSIONS));\n\n\n        private final String saslName;\n        private final String nonce;\n        private final String authorizationId;\n        private final ScramExtensions extensions;\n        public ClientFirstMessage(byte[] messageBytes) throws SaslException {\n            String message = toMessage(messageBytes);\n            Matcher matcher = PATTERN.matcher(message);\n            if (!matcher.matches())\n                throw new SaslException(\"Invalid SCRAM client first message format: \" + message);\n            String authzid = matcher.group(\"authzid\");\n            this.authorizationId = authzid != null ? authzid : \"\";\n            this.saslName = matcher.group(\"saslname\");\n            this.nonce = matcher.group(\"nonce\");\n            String extString = matcher.group(\"extensions\");\n\n            this.extensions = extString.startsWith(\",\") ? new ScramExtensions(extString.substring(1)) : new ScramExtensions();\n        }\n        public ClientFirstMessage(String saslName, String nonce, Map<String, String> extensions) {\n            this.saslName = saslName;\n            this.nonce = nonce;\n            this.extensions = new ScramExtensions(extensions);\n            this.authorizationId = \"\"; //  }\n        public String authorizationId() {\n            return authorizationId;\n        }\n        public String gs2Header() {\n            return \"n,\" + authorizationId + \",\";\n        }\n Utils.mkString(extensions.map(), \"\", \"\", \"=\", \",\");\n\n            if (extensionStr.isEmpty())\n                return String.format(\"n=%s,r=%s\", saslName, nonce);\n            else\n }\n\n    /**\n     * Format:\n     *     [reserved-mext \",\"] nonce \",\" salt \",\" iteration-count [\",\" extensions]\n     * Limitations:\n     *     Extensions are ignored.\n     *\n     */\n \"%sr=(?<nonce>%s),s=(?<salt>%s),i=(?<iterations>[0-9]+)%s\",\n                RESERVED,\n                PRINTABLE,\n                BASE64,\n                EXTENSIONS));\n\n        private final SaslException(\"Invalid SCRAM server first message format: invalid iterations \" + iterations);\n            } catch (NumberFormatException e) {\n                throw new SaslException(\"Invalid + serverNonce;\n            this.salt = salt;\n            this.iterations = iterations;\n        }\n        public String nonce() {\n            return nonce;\n        }\n        public byte[] salt() {\n            return salt;\n        }\n        public int iterations() {\n            return iterations;\n        }\n        String toMessage() {\n            return String.format(\"r=%s,s=%s,i=%d\", nonce, Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(salt), iterations);\n        }\n    }\n    /**\n     * Format:\n     *     channel-binding \",\" nonce [\",\" extensions]\",\" proof\n     * Limitations:\n     *     Extensions are ignored.\n     *\n     */\n    public static class ClientFinalMessage extends AbstractScramMessage {\n        private static final Pattern PATTERN = Pattern.compile(String.format(\n                \"c=(?<channel>%s),r=(?<nonce>%s)%s,p=(?<proof>%s)\",\n                BASE64,\n                PRINTABLE,\n                EXTENSIONS,\n                BASE64));\n\n        private final byte[] channelBinding;\n        private final String nonce;\n        private byte[] proof;\n        public ClientFinalMessage(byte[] messageBytes) throws matcher.group(\"nonce\");\n            this.proof = Base64.getDecoder().decode(matcher.group(\"proof\"));\n        }\n        public ClientFinalMessage(byte[] channelBinding, String nonce) {\n            this.channelBinding = channelBinding;\n            this.nonce = nonce;\n        }\n        public byte[] channelBinding() {\n            return channelBinding;\n        }\n        public String      nonce);\n        }\n        String toMessage() {\n            return String.format(\"%s,p=%s\",\n                    clientFinalMessageWithoutProof(),\n        this.error = error;\n            this.serverSignature = serverSignature;\n        }\n        public String error() {\n            return error;\n        }\n        public byte[] The {@link KafkaPrincipalBuilder} interface\n    27→ * is used when you need to derive a different principal type from the authentication context, or when\n    28→ * you need to represent relations between different principals. The future returned by {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}\n    54→ *       for each listener must return only when authorizer is ready to authorize requests on the listener.</li>\n    55→ *   <li>Broker accepts connections. For each connection, broker performs authentication and then accepts Kafka requests.\n    56→ *       For each request, broker invokes {@link #authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List)} to authorize\n    57→ *       actions performed by the request.</li>\n    58→ * </ol>\n    59→ *\n    60→ * Authorizer implementation class may optionally implement @{@link org.apache.kafka.common.Reconfigurable}\n    61→ * to enable dynamic reconfiguration without restarting the broker.\n    62→ * <p>Authorizer implementation class may also optionally implement {@link org.apache.kafka.common.metrics.Monitorable}\n    63→ * to enable the authorizer to register metrics. The following tags are automatically added to all metrics registered:\n    64→ * <code>config</code> set to <code>authorizer.class.name</code>, <code>class</code> set to the Authorizer class name,\n    65→ * and <code>role</code> set to either <code>broker</code> or <code>controller</code>.\n    66→ * <p>\n    67→ * <b>Threading model:</b>\n    68→ * <ul>\n    69→ *   <li>All authorizer operations including authorization and ACL updates must be thread-safe.</li>\n    70→ *   <li>ACL update methods are asynchronous. This enables\n    75→ *       the caller to process other requests on the request threads without blocking.</li>\n    76→ *   <li>Any threads or thread pools used for processing remote operations asynchronously can be started during\n    77→ *       {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}. }};\n   208→        EnumMap<PatternType, Set<String>> allowPatterns =\n   209→            new EnumMap<>(PatternType.class) {{\n   210→                    put(PatternType.LITERAL, new HashSet<>());\n   211→                    put(PatternType.PREFIXED, new HashSet<>());\n   212→                }};\n   213→\n   214→        boolean hasWildCardAllow = false;\n   215→\n   216→        KafkaPrincipal                && !binding.entry().principal().equals(\"User:*\"))\n   227→                continue;\n   228→\n   229→            if (binding.entry().operation() != op\n   230→                    && denyPatterns.get(PatternType.LITERAL).add(binding.pattern().name());\n   240→                        break;\n   241→                    case PREFIXED:\n   242→                        denyPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).add(binding.pattern().name());\n   243→                        break;\n   244→                    default:\n   245→                }\n   246→                continue;\n   247→            }\n   248→\n   249→            if (binding.entry().permissionType() != AclPermissionType.ALLOW)\n   250→                continue;\n   251→\n   252→            switch        hasWildCardAllow = true;\n   256→                        continue;\n   257→                    }\n   258→                    allowPatterns.get(PatternType.LITERAL).add(binding.pattern().name());\n   259→                    break;\n   260→                case PREFIXED:\n   261→                    allowPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).add(binding.pattern().name());\n   262→                    break;\n   263→                default:\n   264→            }\n   265→        }\n   266→\n   267→ denied, return allow.\n   272→        // For any prefix allowed, if there's no dominant prefix denied, return allow.\n   273→        for (Map.Entry<PatternType, Set<String>> entry : allowPatterns.entrySet()) {\n   274→            for (String allowStr : entry.getValue()) {\n   275→                if (entry.getKey() == PatternType.LITERAL\n   276→                        && 286→                }\n   287→                if (!hasDominatedDeny)\n   288→                    return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED;\n   289→            }\n   290→        }\n   291→\n   292→ Authorizer implementation starts loading its metadata.</li>\n *   <li>Broker starts SocketServer to accept connections and process requests.</li>\n *   <li>For each listener, SocketServer waits for authorization metadata to be available in the\n *       authorizer before accepting connections. The future returned by {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}\n *       for each listener must return only when authorizer is ready to authorize requests on the listener.</li>\n *   <li>Broker accepts connections. For each connection, broker performs authentication and then accepts Kafka requests.\n *       For each request, broker invokes {@link #authorize(AuthorizableRequestContext, List)} to authorize\n *       actions performed by the request.</li>\n * </ol>\n *\n * Authorizer implementation class may optionally implement @{@link org.apache.kafka.common.Reconfigurable}\n * to enable dynamic reconfiguration without restarting the broker.\n * <p>Authorizer implementation class may also optionally implement {@link org.apache.kafka.common.metrics.Monitorable}\n * to enable the authorizer to register metrics. The following tags are automatically added to all metrics registered:\n * <code>config</code> set to <code>authorizer.class.name</code>, <code>class</code> set to the Authorizer class name,\n * and <code>role</code> set to either <code>broker</code> or <code>controller</code>.\n * <p>\n * <b>Threading model:</b>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>All authorizer operations including authorization and ACL updates must be thread-safe.</li>\n *   <li>ACL update methods are asynchronous. Implementations with low update latency may return a\n *       completed future using {@link java.util.concurrent.CompletableFuture#completedFuture(Object)}.\n *       This ensures that the request will be handled synchronously by the caller without using a\n *       purgatory to wait for the result. If ACL updates require remote communication which may block,\n *       return a future that is completed asynchronously when the remote operation completes. This enables\n *       the caller to process other requests on the request threads without blocking.</li>\n *   <li>Any threads or thread pools used for processing remote operations asynchronously can be started during\n *       {@link #start(AuthorizerServerInfo)}. These threads must be shutdown during {@link Authorizer#close()}.</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n */\npublic interface Authorizer extends Configurable, Closeable {\n\n    /**\n     * Starts loading authorization metadata and returns futures that can be used to wait until\n     * metadata for authorizing requests on each listener is available. Each listener will be\n     * started only after its metadata is available and authorizer is ready to start authorizing\n     * requests on that listener.\n     *\n     * @param serverInfo Metadata for the broker including broker id and listener endpoints\n     * @return CompletionStage for each endpoint that completes when authorizer is ready to\n     *         start authorizing requests on that listener.\n     */\n    Map<Endpoint, ? extends CompletionStage<Void>> start(AuthorizerServerInfo serverInfo);\n\n    /**\n     * Authorizes the specified action. Each result is returned as a\n     *         CompletionStage that completes when the result is available.\n     */\n    List<? extends CompletionStage<AclDeleteResult>> deleteAcls(AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext, List<AclBindingFilter> aclBindingFilters);\n\n    /**\n     * Returns ACL bindings which match the provided filter.\n     * <p>\n     * This is a synchronous API designed for use with locally cached ACLs. The default implementation iterates all AclBindings multiple times, without any caching\n     *    by principal, host, operation, permission types, and resource types. More efficient\n     *    implementations may be added in custom authorizers that directly access cached entries.\n     * 2. The default implementation cannot integrate with any audit logging included in the\n     *    authorizer implementation.\n     * 3. The default implementation does not support any custom authorizer configs or other access\n     *    rules apart from ACLs.\n     *\n     * @param requestContext Request context including request resourceType, security protocol and listener name\n     * @param op             The ACL operation to check\n     * @param resourceType   The resource type to check\n     * @return               Return {@link AuthorizationResult#ALLOWED} if the caller is authorized\n     *                       to perform the given ACL operation on at least one resource of the\n     *                       given type. Return {@link AuthorizationResult#DENIED} otherwise.\n     */\n    default AuthorizationResult authorizeByResourceType(AuthorizableRequestContext requestContext, AclOperation op, ResourceType resourceType) {\n        SecurityUtils.authorizeByResourceTypeCheckArgs(op, resourceType);\n\n        // Check a hard-coded name to ensure that super users are granted\n        // access regardless of DENY ACLs.\n        if (authorize(requestContext, Collections.singletonList(new Action(\n                op, new ResourcePattern(resourceType, \"hardcode\", PatternType.LITERAL),\n                0, true, false)))\n                .get(0) == AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED) {\n            return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED;\n        }\n\n        // Filter out all the resource pattern corresponding to the RequestContext,\n        // AclOperation, and ResourceType\n        ResourcePatternFilter resourceTypeFilter = new ResourcePatternFilter(\n            resourceType, null, PatternType.ANY);\n        AclBindingFilter aclFilter = new AclBindingFilter(\n            resourceTypeFilter, AccessControlEntryFilter.ANY);\n\n        EnumMap<PatternType, Set<String>> denyPatterns =\n            new EnumMap<>(PatternType.class) {{\n                    put(PatternType.LITERAL, new HashSet<>());\n                    put(PatternType.PREFIXED, new HashSet<>());\n                }};\n        EnumMap<PatternType, Set<String>> allowPatterns =\n            new EnumMap<>(PatternType.class) {{\n                    put(PatternType.LITERAL, new HashSet<>());\n                    put(PatternType.PREFIXED, new HashSet<>());\n                }};\n\n        boolean hasWildCardAllow = false;\n\n        KafkaPrincipal principal = new KafkaPrincipal(\n            requestContext.principal().getPrincipalType(),\n            requestContext.principal().getName());\n        String hostAddr = requestContext.clientAddress().getHostAddress();\n\n        for (AclBinding binding : acls(aclFilter)) {\n            if (!binding.entry().host().equals(hostAddr) && !binding.entry().host().equals(\"*\"))\n                continue;\n\n            if (!SecurityUtils.parseKafkaPrincipal(binding.entry().principal()).equals(principal)\n                    && !binding.entry().principal().equals(\"User:*\"))\n                continue;\n\n            if (binding.entry().operation() != op\n                    && binding.entry().operation() != AclOperation.ALL)\n                continue;\n\n            if (binding.entry().permissionType() == AclPermissionType.DENY) {\n                switch (binding.pattern().patternType()) {\n                    case LITERAL:\n                        // If wildcard deny exists, return deny directly\n                        if (binding.pattern().name().equals(ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE))\n                            return AuthorizationResult.DENIED;\n                        denyPatterns.get(PatternType.LITERAL).add(binding.pattern().name());\n                        break;\n                    case PREFIXED:\n                        denyPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).add(binding.pattern().name());\n                        break;\n                    default:\n                }\n                continue;\n            }\n\n            if (binding.entry().permissionType() != AclPermissionType.ALLOW)\n                continue;\n\n            switch (binding.pattern().patternType()) {\n                case LITERAL:\n                    if (binding.pattern().name().equals(ResourcePattern.WILDCARD_RESOURCE)) {\n                        hasWildCardAllow = true;\n                        continue;\n                    }\n                    allowPatterns.get(PatternType.LITERAL).add(binding.pattern().name());\n                    break;\n                case PREFIXED:\n                    allowPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).add(binding.pattern().name());\n                    break;\n                default:\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (hasWildCardAllow) {\n            return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED;\n        }\n\n        // For any literal allowed, if there's no dominant literal and prefix denied, return allow.\n        // For any prefix allowed, if there's no dominant prefix denied, return allow.\n        for (Map.Entry<PatternType, Set<String>> entry : allowPatterns.entrySet()) {\n            for (String allowStr : entry.getValue()) {\n                if (entry.getKey() == PatternType.LITERAL\n                        && denyPatterns.get(PatternType.LITERAL).contains(allowStr))\n                    continue;\n                StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();\n                boolean hasDominatedDeny = false;\n                for (char ch : allowStr.toCharArray()) {\n                    sb.append(ch);\n                    if (denyPatterns.get(PatternType.PREFIXED).contains(sb.toString())) {\n                        hasDominatedDeny = true;\n                        break;\n                    }\n                }\n                if (!hasDominatedDeny)\n                    return AuthorizationResult.ALLOWED;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return AuthorizationResult.DENIED;\n    }\n\n}\n","numLines":296,"startLine":1,"totalLines":296}}}

{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-sonnet-4-6","id":"msg_016B4czG6KamzK1PRVWPaD1v","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I have enough information to write a comprehensive analysis. Let me compile the findings:\n\n1. **Entry Points**: \n   - `SaslServerAuthenticator.authenticate()` - receives raw bytes from network\n   - Specifically `handleKafkaRequest()` for handshake/version negotiation\n   - `handleSaslToken()` for SASL mechanism exchanges\n\n2. **Channel Builder Architecture**:\n   - `ChannelBuilders.serverChannelBuilder()` → creates `SaslChannelBuilder`\n   - `SaslChannelBuilder.buildChannel()` → creates `KafkaChannel` with `SaslServerAuthenticator`\n   - During configuration, callback handlers are registered for each SASL mechanism—Plain, Scram, OAuth Bearer, and GSSAPI\n\n3. **SASL Handshake Protocol**:\n   - The initial request can be either `ApiVersionsRequest` or `SaslHandshakeRequest`\n   - After receiving a valid Kafka request, the flow moves to handshake or version negotiation\n   - Following ApiVersions, the next request must be a `SaslHandshakeRequest`\n   - Then the mechanism-specific token exchange happens via `SaslServer.evaluateResponse()` until authentication completes\n\n4. **PLAIN mechanism**:\n   - The client sends credentials as NUL-delimited fields with optional authorization ID\n   - The server parses these fields and invokes the callback handler to authenticate the username and password\n   - Password comparison uses constant-time comparison to prevent timing attacks\n   - The username is set as the authorization ID\n\n5. **SCRAM mechanism**:\n   - This uses a three-message exchange between client and server\n   - The server processes each state transition through `ScramSaslServer.evaluateResponse()`\n   - The callback handler retrieves stored credentials and verifies the client's proof using HMAC-SHA256 with constant-time comparison\n\n6. **OAUTHBEARER**:\n   - The client sends a JWT bearer token which the server parses\n   - Validation is delegated to a callback handler that checks the JWT\n   - The principal name from the token becomes the authorization ID\n\n7. **GSSAPI/Kerberos**:\n   - The server callback handler manages GSSAPI authentication through the JVM's built-in support\n   - Authorization is automatically granted with the authentication ID becoming the authorization ID\n   - The principal builder then applies Kerberos short naming rules to transform the name\n\n8. **Principal Extraction**:\n   - When extracting the principal, the authenticator calls the principal builder which retrieves the authorization ID from the SASL server\n   - For Kerberos, short naming transformations are applied; for SCRAM with token auth, the token authentication flag is set\n   - The result is a KafkaPrincipal with the appropriate type and transformed authorization ID\n\n9. **ACL Authorization**:\n   - Each request triggers an authorization check that matches the principal against stored ACLs\n   - The authorizer evaluates whether the principal has permission for the requested actions\n\nNow looking at the security implications, I'm identifying several potential issues. PLAIN mechanism sends credentials in cleartext unless SASL_SSL is enforced, which is a design concern. More critically, the authorization ID in PLAIN comes directly from the client-provided username without sufficient validation, meaning the client essentially controls what principal name is used for authorization decisions. There's a check for empty credentials, but the username itself becomes the principal with minimal sanitization.\n\nFor SCRAM, the iteration count is properly validated server-side, so that's not exploitable. However, the authorization ID derivation from the client's SASL name in the GS2 header has incomplete validation—while it should match the username or be empty, the enforcement might not catch all edge cases where a client tries to impersonate a different user.\n\nThe OAUTHBEARER mechanism presents a critical vulnerability: by default it uses the unsecured validator that accepts self-signed JWTs without verifying signatures, meaning any client can forge tokens and authenticate as anyone unless operators explicitly configure the proper validator.\n\nThere's also a potential injection issue with how client-supplied software name and version fields are handled in the API versions request.\n\nAdditionally, there's a configurable buffer size limit for SASL authentication to prevent resource exhaustion, and the mechanism negotiation lacks downgrade protection—a MITM could potentially force a client to use a weaker mechanism if multiple options are enabled.\n\nFor GSSAPI, the authorization callback always approves access without validation, relying entirely on the underlying Kerberos authentication. The principal name gets transformed by `KerberosShortNamer`, but if that's not configured, the full Kerberos principal is used directly, which could lead to ACL mismatches. There's also a check to ensure the principal doesn't change during re-authentication.\n\nSCRAM uses a cryptographically secure random nonce generator for the server side. PLAIN has some information leakage in its error messages that distinguish between missing usernames and invalid credentials, but the server masks these with a generic error when responding to clients.
